                        <div data-reactid="1057">
                         Located in prestigious North San Gabriel, Remodeled in 2014, our Solar Safari Trek RV guest home is perfect for couples or families! All the comforts of home! AC/Heat, LED lights, kitchen, refrigerator, range, oven, bathroom w/flush toilet &amp; shower.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1058">
                         Located in prestigious North San Gabriel, our remodeled Solar Safari Trek eco friendly guest home is perfect for couples or a family getaway! All the comforts of home! AC/Heat, All LED lights, kitchen, refrigerator, gas range, oven, bathroom w/flush toilet &amp; shower. Low impact green living at its best! Our RV is solar powered and recently remodeled in 2015 with eco friendly premium materials such as bamboo flooring, brushed nickel fixtures, flat screen TV and granite countertops. This is the much sought after Safari Trek with hidden Electro-Majic queen bed! This means living floor space of a 36ft RV in a 26ft length. This super comfy Queen size memory foam bed with luxury weight bedding stores inside the ceiling to give a large living area and an additional sleeper couch. We also can also provide an extra queen aerobed on request which fits next to the sleeper couch to sleep 6 people (4 adults on the two queens and up to 2 kids or less than 6' individual on the fold out couch) It is a very cozy fit with 6 people but we've personally made it work many times even with 8 people. The classic charm of our 1950's ranch style home and the surrounding homes makes for a wonderful neighborhood to take a relaxing walk or bike. Our Green powered RV guest home is 1 block away and walking distance from some of the most top yelp rated restaurants, trader joes, numerous cafes and only 5 miles away from some of the nicest hiking locations in all of Los Angeles county. We ask you please return the RV to its cleaned state prior to checking out. Don't want to clean? No worries, notify us ahead of time and we'll take care of the cleaning after your departure for a nominal $75 fee. Refundable cleaning/damage deposit taken by airbnb is taken for this purpose.
